# Diplo Action: Buy province from a neighbor country (no subjects except tributary states)
buy_prov_neighbor = {
	category = economy

	alert_index = 12
	alert_tooltip = buy_prov_neighbor_tooltip

	require_acceptance = yes # Whether the recipient gets an option to decline

	is_visible = {
		ai = no
		OR = {
			is_subject = no
			is_subject_of_type = tributary_state
		}
		FROM = {
			ai = yes
		}
	}
	is_allowed = {
		hidden_trigger = {
			ai = no
			OR = {
				is_subject = no
				is_subject_of_type = tributary_state
			}
			FROM = {
				ai = yes
			}
		}
        NOT = {
            has_country_modifier = countdown_next_buy_prov
        }
		treasury = 500
		custom_trigger_tooltip = {
			tooltip = IS_NEIGHBOR_OF_FROM
            # Can buy if:
			OR = {
                # We are neighbors of the target
				is_neighbor_of = FROM
                # Or both we and the target have a port
                AND = {
                    FROM = {
                        any_owned_province = {
                            has_port = yes
                        }
                    }
                    any_owned_province = {
                        has_port = yes
                    }
                }
                # Or any subject country is:
				any_subject_country = {
					OR = {
                        # a neighbor of the target
						is_neighbor_of = FROM

                        # or both the subject and the target have a port
                        AND = {
                            any_owned_province = {
                                has_port = yes
                            }
                            FROM = {
                                any_owned_province = {
                                    has_port = yes
                                }
                            }
                        }
					}
				}
			}
		}
	
	}
	on_accept = {
		set_country_flag = asked_to_buy_province
		set_global_flag = player_bought_province

		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					has_country_modifier = countdown_sold_prov
				}
			}
			set_variable = { which = amount_of_ducats_to_pay_extra value = 0 }
			export_to_variable = {
				which = amount_of_ducats_to_pay_extra
				value = trigger_value:years_of_income
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					FROM = {
						OR = {
							num_of_cities = 30
							variable_arithmetic_trigger = {
								custom_tooltip = COMPARE_NUM_OF_PROVS
								export_to_variable = {
									which = our_num_of_provs
									value = trigger_value:num_of_cities
								}
								export_to_variable = {
									which = their_num_of_provs
									value = trigger_value:num_of_cities
									who = ROOT
								}
								divide_variable = { which = their_num_of_provs value = 2 }
								NOT = { check_variable = { which = our_num_of_provs which = their_num_of_provs } }
							}
						}
					}
				}
				multiply_variable = { which = amount_of_ducats_to_pay_extra value = 3 }
				add_years_of_income = -3
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					FROM = {
						OR = {
							AND = {
								num_of_cities = 20
								NOT = { num_of_cities = 30 }
							}
							variable_arithmetic_trigger = {
								custom_tooltip = COMPARE_NUM_OF_PROVS
								export_to_variable = {
									which = our_num_of_provs
									value = trigger_value:num_of_cities
								}
								export_to_variable = {
									which = their_num_of_provs
									value = trigger_value:num_of_cities
									who = ROOT
								}
								divide_variable = { which = their_num_of_provs value = 3 }
								NOT = { check_variable = { which = our_num_of_provs which = their_num_of_provs } }
							}
						}
					}
				}
				multiply_variable = { which = amount_of_ducats_to_pay_extra value = 4 }
				add_years_of_income = -4
			}
			else = {
				multiply_variable = { which = amount_of_ducats_to_pay_extra value = 5 }
				add_years_of_income = -5
			}
			FROM = {
				set_variable = { which = amount_of_ducats_to_pay_extra which = ROOT }
				while = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { which = amount_of_ducats_to_pay_extra value = 100000 }
					}
					change_variable = { which = amount_of_ducats_to_pay_extra value = -100000 }
					add_treasury = 100000
				}
				while = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { which = amount_of_ducats_to_pay_extra value = 10000 }
					}
					change_variable = { which = amount_of_ducats_to_pay_extra value = -10000 }
					add_treasury = 10000
				}
				while = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { which = amount_of_ducats_to_pay_extra value = 1000 }
					}
					change_variable = { which = amount_of_ducats_to_pay_extra value = -1000 }
					add_treasury = 1000
				}
				while = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { which = amount_of_ducats_to_pay_extra value = 100 }
					}
					change_variable = { which = amount_of_ducats_to_pay_extra value = -100 }
					add_treasury = 100
				}
				while = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { which = amount_of_ducats_to_pay_extra value = 10 }
					}
					change_variable = { which = amount_of_ducats_to_pay_extra value = -10 }
					add_treasury = 10
				}
				while = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { which = amount_of_ducats_to_pay_extra value = 1 }
					}
					change_variable = { which = amount_of_ducats_to_pay_extra value = -1 }
					add_treasury = 1
				}
				while = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { which = amount_of_ducats_to_pay_extra value = 0.1 }
					}
					change_variable = { which = amount_of_ducats_to_pay_extra value = -0.1 }
					add_treasury = 0.1
				}
				while = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { which = amount_of_ducats_to_pay_extra value = 0.01 }
					}
					change_variable = { which = amount_of_ducats_to_pay_extra value = -0.01 }
					add_treasury = 0.01
				}
				set_variable = { which = amount_of_ducats_to_pay_extra value = 0 }
			}
			hidden_effect = { set_variable = { which = amount_of_ducats_to_pay_extra value = 0 } }
		}

		hidden_effect = {	# Just to be sure that flags are removed, before event triggers
			every_province = {
				limit = {
					has_province_flag = counted_as_possible_province
				}
				clr_province_flag = counted_as_possible_province
			}
			every_province = {
				limit = {
					has_province_flag = possible_province
				}
				clr_province_flag = possible_province
			}
			every_province = {
				limit = {
					has_province_flag = already_rejected_prov
				}
				clr_province_flag = already_rejected_prov
			}
		}

		FROM = { country_event = { id = buy_prov_events.1 } }
	}
	on_decline = {
		# No Effect
	}
	ai_acceptance = {
		# Base Value
		add_entry = {
			name = BASE_RELUCTANCE
			export_to_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 20
			}
			multiply_variable = { which = ai_value value = -1 }
		}
		# Negative Values
		add_entry = {
			name = ALL_NEIGHBOR_PROVINCES_ARE_STATES
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					NOT = {
						any_owned_province = {
							is_core = owner
							is_state = no
							OR = {
								any_neighbor_province = {
									owned_by = ROOT
								}
								sea_zone = {
									any_neighbor_province = {
										owned_by = ROOT
									}
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			export_to_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 15
			}
			multiply_variable = { which = ai_value value = -1 }
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = ALREADY_SOLD_10_PROVS_TO_OVERLORD
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					is_subject_of = ROOT
					check_variable = { which = sold_prov value = 10 }
				}
			}
			export_to_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 1000
			}
			multiply_variable = { which = ai_value value = -1 }
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = FROM_HAS_MORE_MONEY_THAN_ROOT
			limit = {
				NOT = { treasury = FROM }
			}
			export_to_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 10
			}
			multiply_variable = { which = ai_value value = -1 }
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = FROM_IS_HRE_MEMBER_BUT_ROOT_NOT
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					is_part_of_hre = yes
				}
				is_part_of_hre = no
			}
			export_to_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 10
			}
			multiply_variable = { which = ai_value value = -1 }
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = FROM_DOES_NOT_NEED_ADM_MONARCH_POWER
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					has_country_modifier = countdown_sold_prov
					adm_power = 800
					OR = {
						AND = {
							NOT = { dip_power = 800 }
							NOT = { mil_power = 800 }
						}
						AND = {
							dip_power = 800
							NOT = { mil_power = 800 }
						}
						AND = {
							NOT = { dip_power = 800 }
							mil_power = 800
						}
					}
				}
			}
			export_to_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 5
			}
			multiply_variable = { which = ai_value value = -1 }
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = FROM_DOES_NOT_NEED_DIP_MONARCH_POWER
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					has_country_modifier = countdown_sold_prov
					dip_power = 800
					OR = {
						AND = {
							NOT = { adm_power = 800 }
							NOT = { mil_power = 800 }
						}
						AND = {
							adm_power = 800
							NOT = { mil_power = 800 }
						}
						AND = {
							NOT = { adm_power = 800 }
							mil_power = 800
						}
					}
				}
			}
			export_to_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 5
			}
			multiply_variable = { which = ai_value value = -1 }
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = FROM_DOES_NOT_NEED_MIL_MONARCH_POWER
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					has_country_modifier = countdown_sold_prov
					mil_power = 800
					OR = {
						AND = {
							NOT = { adm_power = 800 }
							NOT = { dip_power = 800 }
						}
						AND = {
							adm_power = 800
							NOT = { dip_power = 800 }
						}
						AND = {
							NOT = { adm_power = 800 }
							dip_power = 800
						}
					}
				}
			}
			export_to_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 5
			}
			multiply_variable = { which = ai_value value = -1 }
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = FROM_DOES_NOT_NEED_MONARCH_POWER
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					has_country_modifier = countdown_sold_prov
					adm_power = 800
					dip_power = 800
					mil_power = 800
				}
			}
			export_to_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 20
			}
			multiply_variable = { which = ai_value value = -1 }
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = NO_CORE_PROV_AT_BORDER
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					any_owned_province = {
						is_core = ROOT
						OR = {
							AND = {
								has_port = yes
								sea_zone = {
									any_neighbor_province = {
										has_port = yes
										owned_by = FROM
										is_core = FROM
									}
								}
							}
							any_neighbor_province = {
								owned_by = FROM
								is_core = FROM
							}
						}
					}
					any_subject_country = {
						is_colonial_nation = yes
						any_owned_province = {
							is_core = PREV
							OR = {
								AND = {
									has_port = yes
									sea_zone = {
										any_neighbor_province = {
											has_port = yes
											owned_by = FROM
											is_core = FROM
										}
									}
								}
								any_neighbor_province = {
									owned_by = FROM
									is_core = FROM
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			export_to_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 1000
			}
			multiply_variable = { which = ai_value value = -1 }
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = FROM_ALREADY_SOLD_PROV
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					has_country_modifier = countdown_sold_prov
				}
			}
			export_to_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 10
			}
			multiply_variable = { which = ai_value value = -1 }
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = FROM_OR_ROOT_IS_AT_WAR
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_at_war = yes
					FROM = { is_at_war = yes }
				}
			}
			export_to_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 1000
			}
			multiply_variable = { which = ai_value value = -1 }
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = BORDER_DISTANCE
			limit = {
				NOT = { is_neighbor_of = FROM }
				NOT = {
					any_owned_province = {
						has_port = yes
						sea_zone = {
							any_neighbor_province = {
								has_port = yes
								owned_by = FROM
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			export_to_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 1000
			}
			multiply_variable = { which = ai_value value = -1 }
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = RIVAL
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_rival = FROM
					is_enemy = FROM
				}
			}
			export_to_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 1000
			}
			multiply_variable = { which = ai_value value = -1 }
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = ATTITUTE_TOWARDS_ROOT
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					OR = {
						ai_attitude = { who = ROOT attitude = attitude_hostile }
						ai_attitude = { who = ROOT attitude = attitude_domineering }
						ai_attitude = { who = ROOT attitude = attitude_overlord }
						ai_attitude = { who = ROOT attitude = attitude_outraged }
						ai_attitude = { who = ROOT attitude = attitude_rivalry }
						ai_attitude = { who = ROOT attitude = attitude_disloyal }
						ai_attitude = { who = ROOT attitude = attitude_rebellious }
					}
				}
			}
			export_to_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 1000
			}
			multiply_variable = { which = ai_value value = -1 }
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = HAS_ONLY_ONE_CORE_PROV
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					NOT = {
						num_of_owned_provinces_with = { value = 2 is_core = FROM }
					}
				}
			}
			export_to_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 1000
			}
			multiply_variable = { which = ai_value value = -1 }
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = FROM_ALREADY_SOLD_5_PROVS
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					check_variable = { which = sold_prov value = 5 }
				}
			}
			export_to_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 10
			}
			multiply_variable = { which = ai_value value = -1 }
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = ROOT_HAS_MORE_PROVS_THEN_FROM
			limit = {
				num_of_cities = FROM
				num_of_cities = 30
			}
			export_to_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 5
			}
			multiply_variable = { which = ai_value value = -1 }
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = HAS_THREATENED_ATTITUDE
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					ai_attitude = { who = ROOT attitude = attitude_threatened }
				}
			}
			export_to_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 5
			}
			multiply_variable = { which = ai_value value = -1 }
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = HAS_PROTECTIVE_ATTITUDE
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					ai_attitude = { who = ROOT attitude = attitude_protective }
				}
			}
			export_to_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 10
			}
			multiply_variable = { which = ai_value value = -1 }
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = FROM_IS_GREAT_POWER_BUT_ROOT_NOT
			limit = {
				has_dlc = "Rights of Man"
				FROM = {
					is_great_power = yes
				}
				is_great_power = no
			}
			export_to_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 10
			}
			multiply_variable = { which = ai_value value = -1 }
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = ARMY_RATIO
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					army_strength = { who = ROOT value = 2 }
					NOT = { army_strength = { who = ROOT value = 5 } }
				}
			}
			export_to_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 5
			}
			multiply_variable = { which = ai_value value = -1 }
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = ARMY_RATIO
			limit = {
				FROM = { army_strength = { who = ROOT value = 5 } }
			}
			export_to_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 10
			}
			multiply_variable = { which = ai_value value = -1 }
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = FLEET_RATIO
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					naval_strength = { who = ROOT value = 2 }
					NOT = { naval_strength = { who = ROOT value = 5 } }
				}
			}
			export_to_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 5
			}
			multiply_variable = { which = ai_value value = -1 }
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = FLEET_RATIO
			limit = {
				FROM = { naval_strength = { who = ROOT value = 5 } }
			}
			export_to_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 10
			}
			multiply_variable = { which = ai_value value = -1 }
		}

		# Positive Values
		add_entry = {
			name = FROM_NEEDS_ADM_MONARCH_POWER
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					has_country_modifier = countdown_sold_prov
					OR = {
						NOT = { adm_power = 50 }
						AND = {
							NOT = { stability = 0 }
							NOT = { adm_power = 150 }
						}
					}
				}
			}
			export_to_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 5
			}
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = FROM_NEEDS_DIP_MONARCH_POWER
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					has_country_modifier = countdown_sold_prov
					OR = {
						NOT = { dip_power = 50 }
						AND = {
							war_exhaustion = 6
							NOT = { dip_power = 150 }
						}
					}
				}
			}
			export_to_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 5
			}
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = FROM_NEEDS_MIL_MONARCH_POWER
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					has_country_modifier = countdown_sold_prov
					NOT = { mil_power = 50 }
				}
			}
			export_to_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 5
			}
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = FROM_IS_BANKRUPT
			limit = {
				FROM = { is_bankrupt = yes }
			}
			export_to_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 100
			}
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = ROOT_DIPLOMATIC_REPUTATION
			export_to_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = modifier:diplomatic_reputation
			}
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = HAS_MARRIAGE
			limit = {
				marriage_with = FROM
			}
			export_to_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 5
			}
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = HAS_SAME_DYNASTY
			limit = {
				dynasty = FROM
			}
			export_to_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 5
			}
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = HAS_ALLIANCE
			limit = {
				alliance_with = FROM
			}
			export_to_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 15
			}
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = FROM_IS_SUBJECT_OF_ROOT
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					is_subject_of = ROOT
					NOT = { liberty_desire = 50 }
				}
			}
			export_to_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 20
			}
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = HAS_LOYAL_ATTITUDE
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					ai_attitude = { who = ROOT attitude = attitude_loyal }
				}
			}
			export_to_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 20
			}
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = HAS_FRIENDLY_ATTITUDE
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					OR = {
						ai_attitude = { who = ROOT attitude = attitude_friendly }
						ai_attitude = { who = ROOT attitude = attitude_allied }
					}
				}
			}
			export_to_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 10
			}
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = HAS_DEFENSIVE_ATTITUDE
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					ai_attitude = { who = ROOT attitude = attitude_defensive }
				}
			}
			export_to_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 5
			}
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = HAS_NEUTRAL_ATTITUDE
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					ai_attitude = { who = ROOT attitude = attitude_neutral }

						export_to_variable = {
							which = num_of_FROM_cities
							value = trigger_value:num_of_cities
						}
						check_variable = { which = sold_prov which = num_of_FROM_cities }
					}
				}
			}
			export_to_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 50
			}
			multiply_variable = { which = ai_value value = -1 }
		}
	}
	ai_will_do = { always = no }
}

# Diplo Action: Buy province from your colonial nation
buy_prov_colonial_nation = {
	category = economy

	alert_index = 12
	alert_tooltip = buy_prov_colonial_nation_tooltip

	require_acceptance = yes # Whether the recipient gets an option to decline

	is_visible = {
		ai = no
		FROM = {
			ai = yes
			is_colonial_nation_of = ROOT
		}
	}
	is_allowed = {
		hidden_trigger = {
			ai = no
			FROM = {
				ai = yes
				is_colonial_nation_of = ROOT
			}
		}
		treasury = 500
		is_at_war = no
		FROM = {
			is_at_war = no
		}
		FROM = {
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = ANY_OWNED_PROVINCE_IN_WRONG_CR
				any_owned_province = {
					province_is_in_wrong_cr = yes
				}
			}
		}
		custom_trigger_tooltip = {
			tooltip = NOT_JUST_HAS_BOUGHT_A_PROVINCE_OF_COLONY
			NOT = { has_country_modifier = countdown_next_buy_prov_of_colony }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = player_bought_province
			}
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = NO_OTHER_PLAYER_BUYS_PROV
				# NOT = { has_global_flag = player_bought_province }
				always = no
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = player_gets_native_support
			}
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = NO_OTHER_PLAYER_GETS_NATIVE_SUPPORT
				# NOT = { has_global_flag = player_gets_native_support }
				always = no
			}
		}
	}
	on_accept = {
		set_country_flag = asked_to_buy_province
		set_global_flag = player_bought_province

		hidden_effect = {	# Just to be sure that flags are removed, before event triggers
			every_province = {
				limit = {
					has_province_flag = counted_as_possible_province
				}
				clr_province_flag = counted_as_possible_province
			}
			every_province = {
				limit = {
					has_province_flag = possible_province
				}
				clr_province_flag = possible_province
			}
			every_province = {
				limit = {
					has_province_flag = already_rejected_prov
				}
				clr_province_flag = already_rejected_prov
			}
		}

		FROM = { country_event = { id = buy_prov_colony_events.1 } }
	}
	on_decline = {
		# No Effect
	}
	ai_acceptance = {
		# Positive Values
		add_entry = {
			name = HAS_LOYAL_ATTITUDE
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					ai_attitude = { who = ROOT attitude = attitude_loyal }
				}
			}
			export_to_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 100
			}
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = HAS_FRIENDLY_ATTITUDE
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					OR = {
						ai_attitude = { who = ROOT attitude = attitude_friendly }
						ai_attitude = { who = ROOT attitude = attitude_allied }
					}
				}
			}
			export_to_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 50
			}
		}
		# Negative Values
		add_entry = {
			name = HAS_DISLOYAL_ATTITUDE
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					ai_attitude = { who = ROOT attitude = attitude_disloyal }
				}
			}
			export_to_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 1000
			}
			multiply_variable = { which = ai_value value = -1 }
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = HAS_REBELLIOUS_ATTITUDE
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					ai_attitude = { who = ROOT attitude = attitude_rebellious }
				}
			}
			export_to_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 1000
			}
			multiply_variable = { which = ai_value value = -1 }
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = HAS_ONLY_ONE_CORE_PROV
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					NOT = {
						num_of_owned_provinces_with = { value = 2 is_core = FROM }
					}
				}
			}
			export_to_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 1000
			}
			multiply_variable = { which = ai_value value = -1 }
		}
	}
	ai_will_do = { always = no }
}

# Diplo Action: Buy province from your personal unions' colonial nation
buy_prov_union_colonial_nation = {
	category = economy

	alert_index = 12
	alert_tooltip = buy_prov_colonial_nation_tooltip

	require_acceptance = yes # Whether the recipient gets an option to decline

	is_visible = {
		ai = no
		FROM = {
			ai = yes
			overlord = {
				junior_union_with = ROOT
			}
			is_colonial_nation = yes
		}
	}
	is_allowed = {
		hidden_trigger = {
			ai = no
			FROM = {
				ai = yes
				overlord = {
					junior_union_with = ROOT
				}
				is_colonial_nation = yes
			}
		}
		treasury = 500
		is_at_war = no
		FROM = {
			is_at_war = no
			overlord = {
				is_at_war = no
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = ANY_OWNED_PROVINCE_IN_WRONG_CR
				any_owned_province = {
					province_is_in_wrong_cr = yes
				}
			}
		}
		custom_trigger_tooltip = {
			tooltip = NOT_JUST_HAS_BOUGHT_A_PROVINCE_OF_COLONY
			NOT = { has_country_modifier = countdown_next_buy_prov_of_colony }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = player_bought_province
			}
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = NO_OTHER_PLAYER_BUYS_PROV
				# NOT = { has_global_flag = player_bought_province }
				always = no
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = player_gets_native_support
			}
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = NO_OTHER_PLAYER_GETS_NATIVE_SUPPORT
				# NOT = { has_global_flag = player_gets_native_support }
				always = no
			}
		}
	}
	on_accept = {
		set_country_flag = asked_to_buy_province
		set_global_flag = player_bought_province

		hidden_effect = {	# Just to be sure that flags are removed, before event triggers
			every_province = {
				limit = {
					has_province_flag = counted_as_possible_province
				}
				clr_province_flag = counted_as_possible_province
			}
			every_province = {
				limit = {
					has_province_flag = possible_province
				}
				clr_province_flag = possible_province
			}
			every_province = {
				limit = {
					has_province_flag = already_rejected_prov
				}
				clr_province_flag = already_rejected_prov
			}
		}

		FROM = { country_event = { id = buy_prov_union_colony_events.1 } }
	}
	on_decline = {
		# No Effect
	}
	ai_acceptance = {

		add_entry = {
			name = HAS_LOYAL_ATTITUDE
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					ai_attitude = { who = overlord attitude = attitude_loyal }
				}
			}
			export_to_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 100
			}
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = HAS_FRIENDLY_ATTITUDE
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					OR = {
						ai_attitude = { who = overlord attitude = attitude_friendly }
						ai_attitude = { who = overlord attitude = attitude_allied }
					}
				}
			}
			export_to_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 50
			}
		}
		# Negative Values
		add_entry = {
			name = HAS_DISLOYAL_ATTITUDE
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					ai_attitude = { who = overlord attitude = attitude_disloyal }
				}
			}
			export_to_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 1000
			}
			multiply_variable = { which = ai_value value = -1 }
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = HAS_REBELLIOUS_ATTITUDE
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					ai_attitude = { who = overlord attitude = attitude_rebellious }
				}
			}
			export_to_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 1000
			}
			multiply_variable = { which = ai_value value = -1 }
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = HAS_ONLY_ONE_CORE_PROV
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					NOT = {
						num_of_owned_provinces_with = { value = 2 is_core = FROM }
					}
				}
			}
			export_to_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 1000
			}
			multiply_variable = { which = ai_value value = -1 }
		}
	}
	ai_will_do = { always = no }
}

# Diplo Action: Buy province from your subject nation (except tributary states)
buy_prov_subject = {
	category = economy

	alert_index = 12
	alert_tooltip = buy_prov_subject_tooltip

	require_acceptance = yes # Whether the recipient gets an option to decline

	is_visible = {
		ai = no
		FROM = {
			ai = yes
			is_subject_of = ROOT
			NOT = { is_subject_of_type = tributary_state }
			is_colonial_nation = no
		}
	}
	is_allowed = {
		hidden_trigger = {
			ai = no
			FROM = {
				ai = yes
				is_subject_of = ROOT
				NOT = { is_subject_of_type = tributary_state }
				is_colonial_nation = no
			}
		}
		treasury = 500
		is_at_war = no
		FROM = {
			is_at_war = no
		}
		custom_trigger_tooltip = {
			tooltip = IS_NEIGHBOR_OF_FROM
			OR = {
				is_neighbor_of = FROM
				any_owned_province = {
					has_port = yes
					sea_zone = {
						any_neighbor_province = {
							has_port = yes
							owned_by = FROM
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		custom_trigger_tooltip = {
			tooltip = NOT_JUST_HAS_BOUGHT_A_PROVINCE_OF_SUBJECT
			NOT = { has_country_modifier = countdown_next_buy_prov_of_subject }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = player_bought_province
			}
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = NO_OTHER_PLAYER_BUYS_PROV
				# NOT = { has_global_flag = player_bought_province }
				always = no
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = player_gets_native_support
			}
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = NO_OTHER_PLAYER_GETS_NATIVE_SUPPORT
				# NOT = { has_global_flag = player_gets_native_support }
				always = no
			}
		}
	}
	on_accept = {
		set_country_flag = asked_to_buy_province
		set_global_flag = player_bought_province

		hidden_effect = {	# Just to be sure that flags are removed, before event triggers
			every_province = {
				limit = {
					has_province_flag = counted_as_possible_province
				}
				clr_province_flag = counted_as_possible_province
			}
			every_province = {
				limit = {
					has_province_flag = possible_province
				}
				clr_province_flag = possible_province
			}
			every_province = {
				limit = {
					has_province_flag = already_rejected_prov
				}
				clr_province_flag = already_rejected_prov
			}
		}

		FROM = { country_event = { id = buy_prov_subject_events.1 } }
	}
	on_decline = {
		# No Effect
	}
	ai_acceptance = {
		# Positive Values
		add_entry = {
			name = HAS_LOYAL_ATTITUDE
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					ai_attitude = { who = ROOT attitude = attitude_loyal }
				}
			}
			export_to_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 100
			}
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = HAS_FRIENDLY_ATTITUDE
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					OR = {
						ai_attitude = { who = ROOT attitude = attitude_friendly }
						ai_attitude = { who = ROOT attitude = attitude_allied }
					}
				}
			}
			export_to_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 50
			}
		}
		# Negative Values
		add_entry = {
			name = HAS_DISLOYAL_ATTITUDE
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					ai_attitude = { who = ROOT attitude = attitude_disloyal }
				}
			}
			export_to_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 1000
			}
			multiply_variable = { which = ai_value value = -1 }
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = HAS_REBELLIOUS_ATTITUDE
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					ai_attitude = { who = ROOT attitude = attitude_rebellious }
				}
			}
			export_to_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 1000
			}
			multiply_variable = { which = ai_value value = -1 }
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = HAS_ONLY_ONE_CORE_PROV
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					NOT = {
						num_of_owned_provinces_with = { value = 2 is_core = FROM }
					}
				}
			}
			export_to_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 1000
			}
			multiply_variable = { which = ai_value value = -1 }
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = ALREADY_SOLD_10_PROVS_TO_OVERLORD
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					check_variable = { which = sold_prov value = 10 }
				}
			}
			export_to_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 1000
			}
			multiply_variable = { which = ai_value value = -1 }
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = NO_CORE_PROV_AT_BORDER
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					any_owned_province = {
						is_core = ROOT
						OR = {
							AND = {
								has_port = yes
								sea_zone = {
									any_neighbor_province = {
										has_port = yes
										owned_by = FROM
										is_core = FROM
									}
								}
							}
							any_neighbor_province = {
								owned_by = FROM
								is_core = FROM
							}
						}
					}
					any_subject_country = {
						is_colonial_nation = yes
						any_owned_province = {
							is_core = PREV
							OR = {
								AND = {
									has_port = yes
									sea_zone = {
										any_neighbor_province = {
											has_port = yes
											owned_by = FROM
											is_core = FROM
										}
									}
								}
								any_neighbor_province = {
									owned_by = FROM
									is_core = FROM
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			export_to_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 1000
			}
			multiply_variable = { which = ai_value value = -1 }
		}
	}
	ai_will_do = { always = no }
}

# Diplo Action: Buy a colonial nation of another country
buy_colonial_nation = {
	category = economy

	alert_index = 12
	alert_tooltip = buy_colonial_nation_tooltip

	require_acceptance = yes # Whether the recipient gets an option to decline

	is_visible = {
		ai = no
		FROM = {
			ai = yes
			is_colonial_nation = yes
			NOT = { is_colonial_nation_of = ROOT }
		}
	}
	is_allowed = {
		hidden_trigger = {
			ai = no
			FROM = {
				ai = yes
				is_colonial_nation = yes
				NOT = { is_colonial_nation_of = ROOT }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					overlord = { ai = no }
				}
			}
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = FROM_OVERLORD_HAS_TO_BE_AI
				always = no
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					overlord = { ai = yes }
				}
			}
			num_of_colonists = 1
			FROM = {
				capital_scope = { has_discovered = ROOT }
			}
			variable_arithmetic_trigger = {
				custom_tooltip = NEEDS_MONEY_THE_CN_IS_WORTH
				export_to_variable = {
					which = current_treasuryVAR
					value = trigger_value:treasury
				}
				export_to_variable = {
					which = colonial_prov_value
					value = trigger_value:num_of_cities
					who = FROM
				}
				multiply_variable = { which = colonial_prov_value value = 100 }
				change_variable = { which = colonial_prov_value value = 1500 }
				OR = {
					check_variable = { which = current_treasuryVAR which = colonial_prov_value }
					AND = {
						check_variable = { which = colonial_prov_value value = 10000 }
						check_variable = { which = current_treasuryVAR value = 10000 }
					}
				}
			}
			is_subject = no
			is_at_war = no
			FROM = {
				is_at_war = no
			}
			FROM = {
				custom_trigger_tooltip = {
					tooltip = DOES_NOT_HAVE_1_5_YEAR_COOLDOWN_CN
					NOT = { has_country_modifier = cooldown_colonial_nation_not_sold }
				}
			}
			FROM = {
				overlord = {
					is_at_war = no
					is_subject = no
				}
			}
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = NOT_JUST_HAS_BOUGHT_A_CN
				NOT = { has_country_modifier = bought_colonial_nation_countdown }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_global_flag = player_bought_province
				}
				custom_trigger_tooltip = {
					tooltip = NO_OTHER_PLAYER_BUYS_PROV
					# NOT = { has_global_flag = player_bought_province }
					always = no
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_global_flag = player_gets_native_support
				}
				custom_trigger_tooltip = {
					tooltip = NO_OTHER_PLAYER_GETS_NATIVE_SUPPORT
					# NOT = { has_global_flag = player_gets_native_support }
					always = no
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					capital_scope = {
						OR = {
							# North America (vanilla)
							colonial_region = colonial_canada
							colonial_region = colonial_eastern_america
							colonial_region = colonial_louisiana
							colonial_region = colonial_california
							colonial_region = colonial_mexico
							colonial_region = colonial_the_carribean

							# South America (vanilla)
							colonial_region = colonial_colombia
							colonial_region = colonial_peru
							colonial_region = colonial_la_plata
							colonial_region = colonial_brazil

							# Oceania (ET colonial regions)
							colonial_region = colonial_australia
							colonial_region = colonial_oceania

							# Africa (ET colonial regions)
							colonial_region = colonial_south_africa
							colonial_region = colonial_zambezi
							colonial_region = colonial_congo
							colonial_region = colonial_east_africa
							colonial_region = colonial_ethiopia
							colonial_region = colonial_sudan
							colonial_region = colonial_central_africa
							colonial_region = colonial_niger
							colonial_region = colonial_ivory_coast
							colonial_region = colonial_mali
							colonial_region = colonial_west_africa
						}
					}
				}
				capital_scope = {
					custom_trigger_tooltip = {
						tooltip = NOT_IN_COLONIAL_REGION
						always = no
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	on_accept = {
		set_country_flag = asked_to_buy_colonial_nation
		set_global_flag = player_bought_province

		export_to_variable = {
			which = money_to_pay_for_cn
			value = trigger_value:num_of_cities
			who = FROM
		}
		multiply_variable = { which = money_to_pay_for_cn value = 100 }
		change_variable = { which = money_to_pay_for_cn value = 1500 }
		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { which = money_to_pay_for_cn value = 10001 } }
			set_variable = { which = money_to_pay_for_cn value = 10000 }
		}
		while = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { which = money_to_pay_for_cn value = 1000 }
			}
			add_treasury = -1000
			change_variable = { which = money_to_pay_for_cn value = -1000 }
			FROM = { overlord = { add_treasury = 1000 } }
		}
		while = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { which = money_to_pay_for_cn value = 100 }
			}
			add_treasury = -100
			change_variable = { which = money_to_pay_for_cn value = -100 }
			FROM = { overlord = { add_treasury = 100 } }
		}

		FROM = {
			overlord = {
				add_opinion = {
					who = ROOT
					modifier = bought_colonial_nation
				}
				reverse_add_opinion = {
					who = ROOT
					modifier = sold_colonial_nation
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						FROM = {
							OR = {
								num_of_owned_provinces_with = {
									value = 15
									is_core = owner
								}
								total_development = 100
								check_variable = { which = cn_tariff_value value = 15 }
							}
						}
					}
					change_variable = { which = num_of_sold_colonial_nations value = 1 }
				}
				country_event = { id = buy_colonial_nation_events.2 }
			}
			capital_scope = { set_province_flag = cn_was_sold_to_@ROOT }
			add_liberty_desire = -100
			clr_country_flag = chosen_colonial_nation
			every_owned_province = {
				remove_core = FROM
				remove_claim = FROM
				add_core = ROOT
				cede_province = ROOT
			}
		}

		add_country_modifier = {
			name = "bought_colonial_nation_countdown"
			duration = 1095
			hidden = yes
		}

		clr_country_flag = asked_to_buy_colonial_nation
		clr_global_flag = player_bought_province
		set_country_flag = bought_a_colonial_nation_flag
	}
	on_decline = {
		FROM = {
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = "cooldown_colonial_nation_not_sold"
				duration = 548
			}
		}
	}
	ai_acceptance = {
		# Negative Values
		add_entry = {
			name = FROM_IS_HIGH_VALUABLE_COLONY
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					NOT = { liberty_desire = 50 }
					overlord = {
						colony = 8
						calc_true_if = {
							all_subject_country = {
								is_colonial_nation = yes
								NOT = { tag = FROM }
								NOT = { liberty_desire = 50 }
								variable_arithmetic_trigger = {
									custom_tooltip = FROM_TARIFF_VALUE
									export_to_variable = {
										which = FROM_cn_tariff_value
										value = monthly_income
										who = FROM
									}
									OR = {
										FROM = { NOT = { tariff_value = 0.01 } }
										FROM = {
											tariff_value = 0.01
											NOT = { tariff_value = 0.02 }
											PREV = { variable_arithmetic_trigger = { multiply_variable = { which = FROM_cn_tariff_value value = 0.01 } } }
										}
										FROM = {
											tariff_value = 0.02
											NOT = { tariff_value = 0.03 }
											PREV = { variable_arithmetic_trigger = { multiply_variable = { which = FROM_cn_tariff_value value = 0.02 } } }
										}
										FROM = {
											tariff_value = 0.03
											NOT = { tariff_value = 0.04 }
											PREV = { variable_arithmetic_trigger = { multiply_variable = { which = FROM_cn_tariff_value value = 0.03 } } }
										}
										FROM = {
											tariff_value = 0.04
											NOT = { tariff_value = 0.05 }
											PREV = { variable_arithmetic_trigger = { multiply_variable = { which = FROM_cn_tariff_value value = 0.04 } } }
										}
										FROM = {
											tariff_value = 0.05
											NOT = { tariff_value = 0.06 }
											PREV = { variable_arithmetic_trigger = { multiply_variable = { which = FROM_cn_tariff_value value = 0.05 } } }
										}
